inter-broker replication protocol is implemented across multiple modules in the apache/kafka repository. The core replication mechanism consists of the following key components:\\n\\n1. **ReplicaFetcherThread (core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/ReplicaFetcherThread.scala)**: The main thread that runs on follower brokers to fetch data from the leader. It extends AbstractFetcherThread and manages the replication of data.\\n\\n2. **AbstractFetcherThread (core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/AbstractFetcherThread.scala)**: Base class for fetcher threads that provides common fetching logic and mechanisms for tracking replica state changes.\\n\\n3. **ReplicaFetcherManager (core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/ReplicaFetcherManager.scala)**: Manages multiple ReplicaFetcherThread instances and coordinates fetching from multiple leaders.\\n\\n4. **AbstractFetcherManager (core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/AbstractFetcherManager.scala)**: Generic base class for managing fetcher threads.\\n\\n5. **LeaderEpochFileCache (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/epoch/LeaderEpochFileCache.java)**: Maintains a cache of (LeaderEpoch => Offset) mappings for epoch-based recovery. This is critical for handling leader failures and ensuring correct truncation points.\\n\\n6. **EpochEntry (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/EpochEntry.java)**: Represents individual epoch entries in the epoch cache.\\n\\n7. **LeaderEpochCheckpointFile (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/checkpoint/LeaderEpochCheckpointFile.java)**: Persists epoch entries to disk for durability.\\n\\n8. **UnifiedLog (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/UnifiedLog.java)**: The log storage implementation that maintains logStartOffset tracking and manages segment files.\\n\\n9. **LogStartOffsetIncrementReason (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/LogStartOffsetIncrementReason.java)**: Enum defining reasons for incrementing the log start offset (e.g., retention policy, log compaction, admin action).\\n\\n10. **LogAppendInfo (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/LogAppendInfo.java)**: Contains metadata about log appends including byte counts and timestamp information.\\n\\n11. **LogLoader (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/LogLoader.java)**: Loads logs from disk during startup and validates epoch files and segments.\\n\\n12. **ProducerStateManager (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/ProducerStateManager.java)**: Maintains producer state snapshots for idempotent producer semantics.\\n\\n13. **Partition (core/src/main/scala/kafka/cluster/Partition.scala)**: Represents a partition and manages its in-sync replicas (ISR) set, handling shrink and expand operations.\\n\\n14. **ReplicaManager (core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/ReplicaManager.scala)**: Central coordinator for replica management, handling fetcher threads and ISR state changes.\\n\\n15. **AlterPartitionManager (core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/AlterPartitionManager.scala)**: Handles asynchronous ISR updates via AlterPartition requests to the controller, supporting both broker-initiated and controller-initiated ISR changes.\\n\\n16. **LocalLeaderEndPoint (core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/LocalLeaderEndPoint.scala)**: End point for fetching from a local leader broker.\\n\\n17. **RemoteLeaderEndPoint (core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/RemoteLeaderEndPoint.scala)**: End point for fetching from a remote leader broker over the network.\\n\\n18. **LeaderEndPoint (server/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/server/LeaderEndPoint.java)**: Interface defining the contract for accessing leader replica data.\\n\\n19. **ReplicaAlterLogDirsThread (core/src/main/java/kafka/server/TierStateMachine.java)**: State machine for managing tiered storage during replication.\\n\\n22. **Replica (core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/DelayedFetch.scala)**: Handles delayed fetch operations waiting for minimum data requirements.\\n\\n27. **DelayedRemoteFetch (core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/DelayedRemoteFetch.scala)**: Handles delayed fetches for tiered storage.\\n\\nThe inter-broker replication protocol works as follows: ReplicaFetcherThread instances run continuously on each broker to fetch data from remote leaders, updating ReplicaState with the current offsets and fetch times. The Partition class manages the ISR set based on these replica states - replicas that are falling behind are shrunk from the ISR, while caught-up replicas are expanded. The AlterPartitionManager coordinates ISR changes with the Kafka controller. The core replication mechanism consists of the following key components:\\n\\n1. **ReplicaFetcherThread (core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/ReplicaFetcherThread.scala)**: The main thread that runs on follower brokers to fetch data from the leader. It extends AbstractFetcherThread and manages the replication of data.\\n\\n2. **AbstractFetcherThread (core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/AbstractFetcherThread.scala)**: Base class for fetcher threads that provides common fetching logic and mechanisms for tracking replica state changes.\\n\\n3. **ReplicaFetcherManager (core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/ReplicaFetcherManager.scala)**: Manages multiple ReplicaFetcherThread instances and coordinates fetching from multiple leaders.\\n\\n4. **AbstractFetcherManager (core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/AbstractFetcherManager.scala)**: Generic base class for managing fetcher threads.\\n\\n5. **LeaderEpochFileCache (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/epoch/LeaderEpochFileCache.java)**: Maintains a cache of (LeaderEpoch => Offset) mappings for epoch-based recovery. This is critical for handling leader failures and ensuring correct truncation points.\\n\\n6. **EpochEntry (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/EpochEntry.java)**: Represents individual epoch entries in the epoch cache.\\n\\n7. **LeaderEpochCheckpointFile (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/checkpoint/LeaderEpochCheckpointFile.java)**: Persists epoch entries to disk for durability.\\n\\n8. **UnifiedLog (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/UnifiedLog.java)**: The log storage implementation that maintains logStartOffset tracking and manages segment files.\\n\\n9. **LogStartOffsetIncrementReason (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/LogStartOffsetIncrementReason.java)**: Enum defining reasons for incrementing the log start offset (e.g., retention policy, log compaction, admin action).\\n\\n10. **LogAppendInfo (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/LogAppendInfo.java)**: Contains metadata about log appends including byte counts and timestamp information.\\n\\n11. **LogLoader (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/LogLoader.java)**: Loads logs from disk during startup and validates epoch files and segments.\\n\\n12. **ProducerStateManager (storage/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/storage/internals/log/ProducerStateManager.java)**: Maintains producer state snapshots for idempotent producer semantics.\\n\\n13. **Partition (core/src/main/scala/kafka/cluster/Partition.scala)**: Represents a partition and manages its in-sync replicas (ISR) set, handling shrink and expand operations.\\n\\n14. **ReplicaManager (core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/ReplicaManager.scala)**: Central coordinator for replica management, handling fetcher threads and ISR state changes.\\n\\n15. **AlterPartitionManager (core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/AlterPartitionManager.scala)**: Handles asynchronous ISR updates via AlterPartition requests to the controller, supporting both broker-initiated and controller-initiated ISR changes.\\n\\n16. **LocalLeaderEndPoint (core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/LocalLeaderEndPoint.scala)**: End point for fetching from a local leader broker.\\n\\n17. **RemoteLeaderEndPoint (core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/RemoteLeaderEndPoint.scala)**: End point for fetching from a remote leader broker over the network.\\n\\n18. **LeaderEndPoint (core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/ReplicaAlterLogDirsThread.scala)**: Thread for managing log directory changes during rebalancing.\\n\\n20. **ReplicaAlterLogDirsManager (core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/ReplicaAlterLogDirsManager.scala)**: Manages ReplicaAlterLogDirsThread instances.\\n\\n21. **TierStateMachine (core/src/main/java/kafka/server/TierStateMachine.java)**: State machine for managing tiered storage during replication.\\n\\n22. **Replica (server/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/server/replica/Replica.java)**: Represents a single replica with metadata.\\n\\n23. **ReplicaState (server/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/server/replica/ReplicaState.java)**: Record tracking the state of a remote replica including logStartOffset, logEndOffset, lastFetchTime, and lastCaughtUpTime - essential for ISR calculations.\\n\\n24. **ReplicationConfigs (server/src/main/java/org/apache/kafka/server/config/ReplicationConfigs.java)**: Configuration parameters for replication behavior.\\n\\n25. **FetchSession (core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/FetchSession.scala)**: Session state for tracking fetch requests from followers.\\n\\n26. **DelayedFetch (core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/DelayedFetch.scala)**: Handles delayed fetch operations waiting for minimum data requirements.\\n\\n27. **DelayedRemoteFetch (core/src/main/scala/kafka/server/DelayedRemoteFetch.scala)**: Handles delayed fetches for tiered storage.\\n\\nThe inter-broker replication protocol works as follows: ReplicaFetcherThread instances run continuously on each broker to fetch data from remote leaders, updating ReplicaState with the current offsets and fetch times. The Partition class manages the ISR set based on these replica states - replicas that are falling behind are shrunk from the ISR, while caught-up replicas are expanded. The AlterPartitionManager coordinates ISR changes with the Kafka controller. LeaderEpochFileCache and related epoch files ensure that followers can recover correctly after failures, using epoch boundaries to determine truncation points rather than just timestamps or broker IDs.\"\n}","stderr":"","interrupted":false,"isImage":false,"noOutputExpected":false}}
